<Text>I only came here for the kimchi pasta, but then I saw the mac and cheese on the menu and I had to try that as well...

The kimchi pasta wasn't worth it. It was actually more dry and oily, not creamy and rich like I expected. I prefer Cafe Gunul's. The pricing was also a bit expensive for the portion.

The mac and cheese, sliders, and tacos were all decent. I'm not a fan of tacos and sliders that are too hard eat and the sliders were too spicy for me, but otherwise pretty good.

Service was really great, even though it looked like there was only one person dealing with all the customers on a weekday evening. Props to her.

Pricing during happy hour: kimchi pasta ($10), spicy pork sliders ($8), spicy pork kbbq taco ($9), mac and cheese ($9).<//Text>< pictures>

< review>
I was referred to this place by my insurance and didn't have many options.  The doctors and assistants are nice enough but the office is tremendously over booked.  It's difficult to tell if the people there cant do their job or they are overworked and/or a combination.  To get a call in is nearly impossible.  If you do get a call in, expect to be on hold for at least 30 minutes or longer.  When you actually show up at the office, your expect to be seen at least 30 minutes after your appointment time but most likely closer to 45-60 minutes.  This is only for your vitals to be taken, then you are sent to a second waiting room to wait for a room to be seen.  A visit that should take no more then 30 minutes takes anywhere between 90-120 minutes.  The doctors there are not there daily, apparently 1-2 days at most so it is very difficult to get an appointment and then to change it is impossible.  If you get sent to get some labworks done, MRI, CT scan, etc make sure to have a copy with you because they never seem to have the results from the labs.  There also appears be bad communication between the doctors because when my staples where to be taken out he did not know if my surgical drain was to be taken out.  I had to wait a couple of hours to see if this was going to be done.  The owners of this medical center need to get more people to work at their location.  Also, they have parking but they never had any parking available and please make sure to have your copay ready because that they do request almost immediately upon checking in with the clinic.< /review>

Benjamin M. was the first to reply to order with an email that they had my car on the floor. I was skeptical since I had customized everything online, and I was right to be because when I got there it was slightly different. The year was a 2019 not a 2020, and the color was black, not blue.

Ben explained that it could take 4-6 months (or longer with COVID delays) to get the 2020 model in, and I knew by that time that the 2021's would be in.

<Text>Running 4 companies doesn't give me a lot of time to write reviews, but I felt compelled to write a review for David Kim at McKenna Audi because of his #WhateverItTakes attitude towards helping me create an awesome experience for my team.

This year I made the decision to reward my top performing Directors with a company car. I didn't want to get them a Honda or Toyota, rather, I wanted them to truly feel appreciated. With that in mind, I chose Audi A4's with the Black Optics kit. Finding (3) identical Audi A4's was no easy task. David Kim came through for me and found the exact vehicle I was looking for, not once, but three (3) times in the short span of one (1) month! (Win #1 for David Kim)

We had some hiccups along the way with VW Credit due to the fact that most companies don't fleet Audi's as much as they do with Toyota. Getting VW Credit to authorize that many vehicles for lease in a 30-day window took some finesse. David Kim worked with the finance team at McKenna, and also escalated our challenge to Danny McKenna who also pulled strings to help close the deal. (Win #2 for David Kim)

With all of the hustle that went into making three (3) identical vehicles available for pick up in the short timeframe we were requesting, there were some paperwork gaps that occurred. David Kim drove to my residence to get the paperwork signed. (Win #3 for David Kim)

With the first A4 I wanted to deliver, it was my goal to surprise my #1 top performer who would be the first recipient of the first vehicle we leased. David Kim drove the car out to my personal residence He not only had the car detailed with Armor All on the tires, but he presented my employee with a nice red box with the keys inside. (Win #4 for David Kim)

I had my next #2 Rockstar employee blown away when I knocked on his door and presented him with the keys to his new Audi A4 with the Black Optics kit and 19-inch wheels). (Win #5 for David Kim)

With my last employee I drove this employee out to the dealership. The wheelset was not the same as the other two vehicles, and that was a big problem for me. The goal with the fleet vehicles was to present each top performer with an awesome incentive that was equal to the other top performers (I didn't want any of them resenting the company because they didn't get the same vehicle as the others - having identical vehicles was critical). David Kim collaborated with Danny McKenna to work with Audi HQ in order to get us the exact same wheelset as the previous two vehicles. When we went to deliver the vehicle to this last employee, David Kim (once again) came out to my personal residence and delivered the vehicle (with the keys inside the cool red box). (Win #6 for David Kim)

Here we are almost nine (9) months after the Audi A4 presentation to my top performers and David Kim, once again, came through for me...and this time, for my wife. We've been considering the Audi Q7 for our primary family vehicle. I called David out of the blue and told him the exact vehicle I was looking for. Within an hour he called me back and told me he had the model, color, and wheelset we wanted. The deal was negotiated over the phone and I simply showed up at the dealership to sign the paperwork and take delivery. (Win #7 for David Kim).

Both, David Kim and Danny McKenna, have come through for me this past year in ways that helped me provide an awesome experience for my team and, personally, with my wife!

I couldn't be more happy with the experience I've had with McKenna Audi and David Kim!

As a key takeaway, if you're looking for a new Audi, McKenna Audi will provide you with the first class experience you would expect with a premium-performance vehicle acquisition!<//Text></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
I have been looking for a great deal on an amazing Audi. I had called several dealerships (Pasadena, Beverly Hills, Riverside, Pacific Auto in Torrance) and they were all about the games. I had one dealership giving me a great deal on the invoice price and then manipulate the money factor to collect the difference on the back end. It was truly "magic" with numbers. Pasadena took 3 days to call me on my online inquiry. I did not even bother with them.

Another dealership had me talking to 4 people because the salesman didn't know the features and packages available on the car and could not explain the "fuzzy" math. It was a confusing process with everyone contradicting themselves.

Thursday night I saw a vehicle with McKenna dealer plates. I totally forgot about this dealership. I did an online inquiry late Thursday night and then Friday morning I got a call from Alex at 830 am!!! I was impressed because the response was fast and he called me before the dealership opened. This was a man that was ready to sell a vehicle.

Now, Alex and I had a very rough start. He was a "fast talker" and didn't appear to get it that I did not want the minutia of sales. I just wanted to get straight to the numbers. I was frustrated and ended the call.

He was very apologetic via text message and did his best to smooth things over. His sales manager Michael also gave me an apology and explained that Alex has good intentions and that he just gets excited.

I gave Alex another chance and he made me a promise that he was going to get me a deal that would make me smile. He went to bat for me and heard my terms and conditions. He explained all the numbers and how they work. He did not oversell me on any additional options. He gave me exactly what I wanted for a deal most people won't even see around Christmas.

If you're looking to deal with an honest salesman that is truly knowledgeable about the business he is the one to work with at Mckenna! I only dealt with him when I arrived because he was knowledgeable and Nicole in finance.

Nicole has a tough job doing the financing for 3 dealerships (BMW, Audi, and Porsche). She got us in and out with the paperwork. She saw my rims and told me of a coverage that I would recommend anyone leasing getting.
I will recommend anyone to deal with McKenna Audi of Norwalk. Alex was the best. He was very patient with an impatient and detailed customer. Thank you for turning around car buying experience!</Review>

I've been coming here for years, but since I moved from Carlsbad, I've been coming less.

I only go during happy hour because you gotta stick to a budget.

The girls that work here are nice. At times, the service is slow, but nothing too major.

I always order cajun wings when I come. This might be the only place im a good eater, because i can eat a whole order, but can't get to 10 nuggies. Life's crazy like that.

We ordered cheese fried as well with the nacho sauce And shrimp cocktail. Everything is tasty!

The special slot if the day was tasty - I believe it was an apple bourbon & I could use more of those in my life!

All in all, good food, decent prices keep bringing me back for more.<//review>

< text>
I stopped in a few weeks ago when I was in town. I was looking for a good beer and some good food to have for lunch and scoped this place out w/o reading any reviews.  "Going in blind..." as they say in the Yelp Universe. It's located in a weird part of a strip mall. If you blink you'll miss it. The inside is MASSIVE, so you won't have a problem finding an open seat.

I walked in and the bartender was the only one working. I saddled up at the end of the bar and waited....and waited....and waited for her to take my drink order. A few minutes later she took my order and gave me a menu. I opted for the Arrogant Bastard and a club sandwich. Let me say that the sandwich...although only a sandwich, was one of the best I've had in a while. Everyone that came in seemed to be fairly satisfied with their grub also.

So the food and beer were good, but the service was a little sparse. I also expect a bartender to strike up some conversation, but this didn't happen. Maybe since she was the only one working, she was busy. Maybe not. If I'm in the mood for another tasty sandwich and brew, I'll def stop by.< /text>

< name>
Lilith Laney< /name>
< date>
1527914315213< /date>
<Rate>5<//Rate>< Text>
This review will be two parts. Food/Drinks, Service/Ambiance&Crowd.
Food/Drinks: Rookies food is delicious, not just for a sports bar either. I've tried a pretty decent selection across the menu and I have almost no qualms with anything. The meat is always properly cooked, when you get it delivered the food never gets soggy quickly and they do not skimp out on sauces or little extras like cheese. The only things that aren't great is that on the all star sampler platter they sometimes only give you literally 2 or 3 pieces of shrimp which is disappointing but it's still a lot of food for only 15$ and will easily feed 2 very hungry people, my other complaint is more personal preference but I don't like crinkle cut fries especially in carne asada fries but it is a sports bar so you can't really expect perfect quality Mexican food. The drinks are pretty standard. They are made well and average priced. The specials they have for beers are amazing if you like domestic beers, personally I like craft and mexican beers but they are still very good priced during happy hour.
Service/Ambiance&Crowd: The servers here are always very friendly and professional. The bartenders are quick and they do not water down drinks. Overall 8/10 when it comes to service, they lost 2 points because they can take a good minute to come clear your table when you're done eating even for the place being packed. My final part for ambiance and crowd is extremely biased. I do not like extremely packed and LOUD places which is how the bar is almost every day past 6 pm. The music and TV's are so loud you have to yell to talk to someone sitting right next to you, I would go so far as to say it is as loud as a club. The live music is good if that's the type of music you like, I personally don't like generic bro rock but if that's your thing you will love it. I am not a sports person nor do I typically like people who are into sports. I'm a goth lady so the crowd that usually frequents here is not my crowd. The groups of straight guys who come in are you stereotypical beer drinking, kind of chauvinistic bros whom I wish did not exist. However, there is usually multiple groups of people from all walks of life. I've seen 2 fights break out and the bouncers handled it quickly, quietly and effectively. It is a huge place which you wouldn't expect from the shopping center it is tucked away in. Definitely a good place for groups of 5+ people.
Overall I give this place 4.3/5 stars. If you like sports you will absolutely love this establishment. As for myself I love the food and order it to be picked up every week on my cheat day. If you don't mind loud crowded bars this place is a must try. If that's not your speed it is still a fun place to try and the food makes it worth while for an introvert like myself.<//Text>

<Text>I felt like a rookie stepping back in here after years. YEARS. Of not coming here. Sure my history with them started as a kid coming here with my parents to do their comedy drivers safety course, then coming here as an underaged adult and then thinking it was all the same to now.

Bravo on the remodel, which probably happened 5 years ago based on general wear. It still has the same layout, but is eerily a lot like The Draft on the upper level. The lower dance floor is filled with line dancing country, latin, top 40, hip hop and live music depending on the night. It’s much brighter and more open. Pool tables up top are given room and the seating areas are only crowded around the big table.

It’s not quite a dive bar anymore, the sports aspect is cool, but I must have come on country night. The smoking area was raging, people coming in and out all night. Blue wrist bands, red wrist bands for of age people. They do their wings night on Tuesday and it’s a steal at $0.50 a wing or 10 for $5. They take some liberty with the flavors, but they also do some customs wet/dry finishes/combos. Margarita Mondays has drinks specials, playing bachata, banda, cumbia, reggeaton, latin. Tuesdays has wings, well specials and country music. Wednesdays is all day HH. $3, $5, $7 menu specials. Thursdays have ½ off food and DJ’s in the evening. Saturday $10 burger and brew special. Basically there is a special every day, super enticing, even industry night.

Burgers are Black Angus Choice, hefty, get the pretzel bun, which I thought was notable. Drinks are basic, nothing craft, but still.

It’s definitely an upgrade and not so bad to lose it’s dive bar image. It’s a place that is sure a hit for people watching.< /Text><Pics>None</Pics><resp>{'time': 1528311529374, 'text': "We love this review!! Thank you so much Walter.
